                        function wpvl_paramReplace(name, string, value) {
                // Find the param with regex
                // Grab the first character in the returned string (should be ? or &)
                // Replace our href string with our new value, passing on the name and delimeter

                var re = new RegExp("[\?&]" + name + "=([^&#]*)");
                var matches = re.exec(string);
                var newString;

                if (matches === null) {
                    // if there are no params, append the parameter
                    newString = string + '?' + name + '=' + value;
                } else {
                    var delimeter = matches[0].charAt(0);
                    newString = string.replace(re, delimeter + name + "=" + value);
                }
                return newString;
            }

            var hideTopMenu = true;

window.onload = function() { 

 // check if it is the main page
 var mainPage = (window.location.href.replace("http://", "").replace("https://", "").split("/").length < 3) || ((window.location.href.replace("http://", "").replace("https://", "").split("/").length < 4) && (window.location.href.indexOf("/pl") != -1) );
 // check if it is the blog page
 var blogPage = false; // (document.body.innerHTML.indexOf("games and tools in Unity3D") == -1);
 // check if it is the portfolio page
 var portfolioPage = false; //  (window.location.href.indexOf("portfolio") != -1);
 // check if it is the mars force landing
 var marsForceLandingPage = false; //  (window.location.href.indexOf("marsforcegame") != -1);
 // check if it is the brc landing
 var brcLandingPage = false; //  (window.location.href.indexOf("brcgame") != -1);
 // check if it is a polish version of the site
 var polishPage= (window.location.href.indexOf("/pl") != -1);
 // check if it is a relacje inwestorskie page
 var relacjePage= (window.location.href.indexOf("relacjeinwestorskie") != -1);
 // check if it is a privacypolicy e page
 var privacypolicyPage = (window.location.href.indexOf("privacypolicy") != -1);

if (privacypolicyPage) return;

if (relacjePage)
{
polishPage = true;
}

// always redirect to the main page
if (!mainPage && !relacjePage) {
   window.location.href = "http://gameboomvr.com";
}

if (marsForceLandingPage || portfolioPage || brcLandingPage  ) {
   blogPage = false;
}

// disable blog
if (blogPage) {
   window.location.href = "http://gameboomvr.com";
}

 // change logo and sentence in the center
 if (!portfolioPage && !marsForceLandingPage && !brcLandingPage ) {
     //document.getElementsByTagName("h1")[0].className = document.getElementsByTagName("h1")[0].className  + " gameboomvrlogo";

     //document.getElementsByTagName("p")[0].style.display= "none";
 }


// show main menu (not on GameBoom VR site)
//TopMenuSwitch();


 if (mainPage) {
    // give ids to sections
    var sections = document.getElementsByTagName("section");
    for (i = 0; i < sections.length; i++)
    {
       sections[i].id = "section" + i;
    }
 }
 else
 {
    // only first section can be clicked on the blog and sub-pages
    document.getElementsByTagName("section")[0].onclick = TopMenuSwitch;
 }

 // remove current page underscores
 var menuMainMenu = document.getElementById("menu-main-menu");
 if (menuMainMenu != null)
 {
  var menuLinks = menuMainMenu.children;
  for (i = 0; i < menuLinks.length; i++) {
     while (menuLinks[i].className.indexOf("active") != -1) {
        menuLinks[i].className =  menuLinks[i].className.replace("active", "");
        menuLinks[i].className =  menuLinks[i].className.replace("current-menu-item", "");
        menuLinks[i].className =  menuLinks[i].className.replace("current_page_item", "");
     }
  }

     // hide relacje link or home link
     if (polishPage)
      {
         menuLinks[0].style.display = "none";  //hide first link in menu - HOME
      }
      else
      {
         menuLinks[2].getElementsByTagName("a")[0].innerHTML = "relacje inwestorskie (in polish)"; // add "(IN POLISH)" to relacje inwestorskie text
      }
 }

 if (mainPage) {
    // change mailto link
    // document.getElementById("section5").getElementsByTagName("a")[0].href = "mailto:contact@gameboomvr.com";

    // show menu when the top of the site clicked
    //document.getElementById("section0").onclick = TopMenuSwitch;  <-- not on GameBoom VR site

    document.getElementById("section0").style.padding = "0 0 72px 0";

    // scroll down when the site is clicked near the bottom half of the screen on laptop
    // document.getElementById("section1").addEventListener('click', function() {
    //    MoveSmoothly("#section1");
    // });

    // add unity badges
    // var portrets = document.getElementsByTagName("figure");

    // var div = document.createElement('div');
    // div.className = "unitybadge";
    // portrets[0].parentNode.appendChild(div);
    // div.onclick = function() { window.open('https://www.youracclaim.com/badges/a4b4402d-ecbf-4262-96fa-a1c975aa5181', '_blank'); };

    // var div2 = document.createElement('div');
    // div2.className = "unitybadge";
    // portrets[1].parentNode.appendChild(div2);
    // div2.onclick = function() { window.open('https://www.youracclaim.com/badges/c9b62936-f694-44db-81f4-c66a99551b1d', '_blank'); };

    // block links with our names
    //var aTags = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
    //for (var i = 0; i < aTags.length; i++) {
    //    if (aTags[i].textContent.indexOf("Krzykwa") >= 0) {
   //         aTags[i].style.cursor = "default";
     //       aTags[i].onclick = function() {return false;};
     //    }
      //  if (aTags[i].textContent.indexOf("Bancewicz") >= 0) {
     //       aTags[i].style.cursor = "default";
     //       aTags[i].onclick = function() {return false;};
     //    }
   // }

 }


 // hide right column in portfolio
 if (portfolioPage) {
    columns = document.getElementsByClassName("col-md-4");
    for (i=0; i < columns.length; i++) {
       if (columns[i].className == "col-md-4") {
          columns[i].style.display = "none";
       }
    }
 }


 // remove unnecessary links (they stay just for coloring purposes)
 if (mainPage) {
    var links = document.getElementsByTagName("a");
    for (i = 1; i < links.length; i++) {
        if (links[i].href == "http://gameboomvr.com/") {
           links[i].onclick = function() { return false;};
        }
    }
 }

 if (portfolioPage) {
    // portfolio items changes
    var figcaptions = document.getElementsByTagName("figcaption");
    for (i = 0; i < figcaptions.length; i++) {
       if (figcaptions[i].className == "") {

          // remove portfolio zoom
          var figcaptionChildren = figcaptions[i].children;
          for (j = 0; j < figcaptionChildren.length; j++) {
             if (figcaptionChildren[j].tagName.toLowerCase() == "a") {
                figcaptionChildren[j].style.display = "none";
                break;
             }
          }

          // add onclick to whole items' graphics
          figcaptions[i].onclick = function() { location.href = this.parentNode.children[0].href;};

          // change cursor
          figcaptions[i].style.cursor = "pointer";
       }
    }
 }


// remove KRS info from pages other than main
if (!mainPage && !relacjePage) {
var krsFooter = document.getElementById("text-4");
    if (krsFooter != null) {
        krsFooter.style.display = "none";
    }
}

// end of onload
}

<article id="post-1056" class="post-1056 page type-page status-publish hentry">
    <p>This is our Privacy Policy.</p>
<p>Please check from time to time whether it has been updated.</p>
<p>This Privacy Policy sets out how we collect, use and disclose “personal information” and other “non personal information”.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>What is Personal Information?</p>
<p>‘Personal Information’ is information or an opinion that identifies you as an individual.</p>
<p>OUR PRINCIPLE IS NO COLLECTION/PROCESSING OF PERSONAL DATA:</p>
<p>We normally do not and will not collect or otherwise process any personal data (whether yours, or any other person’s), even when you purchase our game(s), play it or use any self-development kit, etc.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>However, your personal data (if any) may be collected and processed by the internet distribution platform wherefrom you purchase our game(s).</p>
<p>Your personal data may also be processed by Unity, which ensures the creation and management of statistics concerning our game as mentioned above. (Privacy policy available at: <a href="https://unity3d.com/legal/privacy-policy">https://unity3d.com/legal/privacy-policy</a>)</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>For any request concerning your personal data, please refer to the terms of service/sale of that internet distribution platform, which must provide you with the contact details of the relevant data protection officer(s).</p>
<p>GameBoom VR has no control over and is not responsible for how your data is being processed by an internet platform.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>Also, if you contact us directly for any reason, we may keep a copy of that correspondence and your email. Your email is collected only to keep you informed of new products and changes to our existing products – we will never pass your email onto third parties.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>ANONYMIZED DATA:</p>
<p>We may decide to collect anonymized information from your play of our game(s).</p>
<p>We would use such information to analyze and improve our game(s) and support our internal operations.</p>
<p>Anonymized information means that it cannot be used to identify any particular player.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>WHAT IF WE HAPPEN TO COLLECT/PROCESS OF PERSONAL DATA?</p>
<p>In the event that GameBoom VR would happen to collect and process personal data with respect to you, the following rules would apply:</p>
<p>Your consent would have to be expressly obtained.</p>
<p>Such a collection and processing of your personal data would have to be necessary for GameBoom VR to either sell you game(s) or provide you other GameBoom VR services. Only that information which is strictly necessary for these purposes would be collected.</p>
<p>GameBoom VR would normally not transfer your personal data to any other person, unless if mandatorily requested to do so by a authority duly entitled to make such a request.</p>
<p>&nbsp;</p>
<p>You can contact us via email: contact@gameboomvr.com</p>
